08 Jan 2017 23:23:06 : LimitlessMc, staff, Botfuzzy77#2209, ** #10616  by Phoenix Mon Jul 25, 2016 2:12 pm 			**
Порно Пиздюхи Видиеоролики 2017
------------------------------------
My suggestions is designated housing nearer to the spawn point where construction of starting structures or "eye sores" is discouraged and the moderators are allowed to deleted unsavory structures after a set amount of time. There are plenty a beautiful structures around the sever currently but they are scattered. A somewhat reserved  area would allow for hopefully active players who take pride in what their homes look like to make a neighborhood of beautiful homes. This would be enjoyable for players to walk through and explore. 

Another variation of this would be to encourage the "Guild" System and give each "Guild" a preset area where players can try to build houses next to each other and the guilds could have common, unclaimed, structures that are for use by everyone. 

I know this suggestion hinges on players actively working together to make these neighborhoods; but I feel that moderator control of designating areas would help this along. My hope is that this will encourage player interaction outside of pokemon battles and selling things.
